\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{triangle-vulkan_8c_source_l00028}00028 \textcolor{comment}{ * Draw a textured triangle with depth testing.  This is written against Intel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{triangle-vulkan_8c_source_l00029}00029 \textcolor{comment}{ * ICD.  It does not do state transition nor object memory binding like it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{triangle-vulkan_8c_source_l00030}00030 \textcolor{comment}{ * should.  It also does no error checking.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{triangle-vulkan_8c_source_l00031}00031 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
